+: The hotel exterior is beautiful. It is well located next to the outlets and the Liupancun Village food street. The beach is 8 min driving. The hotel is not new but clean. The view from the room is great and you can hear the birds in the morning! The pool is good. 

-: The breakfast is mainly local Chinese food with almost no variety of western food besides bread and fruit. 
- The room is not spacious for 2 people - not enough luggage space room to open and use your luggage. 
- There are animals on the territory of the hotel (llamas, alpacas, peacocks and even a dear). It might be fun for children but definitely not good for those animals(

Overall, the the hotel is nice and cost effective.
